Selected Speeches of Reverend Sun Myung Moon

Compiled by the Editorial Committee of Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Speeches

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Reverend Sun Myung Moon, who received the calling for the salvation of humanity from Heaven at the age of 16, has lived his entire life centered on the Heavenly Way with a single-minded devotion. He described his life as follows:
"If Reverend Moon has any wealth, it is nothing but the suffering endured for the public rather than for myself. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I also tried to suffer more than anyone else. …… Reverend Moon has received countless opposition and persecution from nations and the world. I was opposed in America, and Christianity, Judaism, and even communists opposed me. In history, there has never been a time when the world united to eliminate one person. In that sense, I might be a world champion. However, despite being cursed, I have not been crushed or destroyed. I have emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. …… Reverend Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the liberation of the spirit world, the liberation of hell, and even the liberation of God." (Refer to the Collected Speeches, Volume 105, pages 101-103)
In short, Reverend Moon's life can be defined as 'suffering itself.' This suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. From this, we come to understand who he is. Reverend Moon is the returning Lord, the savior, and the true parent of humanity that Christianity has hoped for over 2000 years. Already, disciples following Reverend Moon in 185 countries around the world are realizing the ideal of a true family with this confession of faith.
Reverend Moon's self-identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humans, history and the world, and the spirit world are clarified in his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled in him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' Moreover, the more important thing is that Reverend Moon's words are merely 'interpretations of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, incarnated. Therefore, life itself is the truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'the Word.'
I am confident that readers will understand his greatness through Reverend Moon's words. Although the depth and height of his words are immeasurable, they fundamentally have three characteristics.
First, Reverend Moon revealed God through his words and life. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the bloodline of evil, they are children but cannot be called children, causing God's suffering. Reverend Moon made the sorrowful God, alienated by human sin, 'speak.' He made God, who was silent in the ornate buildings of ecclesiastical authority and doctrine, 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as a parent, 'become a parent,' making Reverend Moon 'the perfect revelation of God.'
Secondly, Reverend Moon liberated humans from ignorance and chaos. Although we humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, we cannot deny the tragic reality that we cannot fully explain our own existence. Furthermore, humans are not independent beings but interdependent beings inseparable from others, yet they have not clarified this relationality. This is because they lost God's words. Reverend Moon provides the ultimate answer to this. Moreover, through a life that upholds the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete path of example. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, Reverend Moon liberated the world of all things. Every object created by God is an individual truth body with inherent value. Although its value should be fully realized under the dominion of the original human of creation, it has not been, causing all things to groan. Reverend Moon clarified the original value of the world of all things through his words and opened the path to the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Reverend Moon and his wife, who have come as the eternal true parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly deliver speeches around the world, demonstrating through their substantial lives the teachings of 'wearing the servant's body with the heart of a parent' and 'living for the sake of others,' and working to bequeath true love, true life, and true lineage.
Additionally, through the words of life, noble life, and achievements, Reverend Moon has finally restored and offered God's sovereignty as we enter the new millennium, settling as the king of blessed families on this earth. He has been acclaimed as the king of peace by peace activists from various fields centered on global politics and religion. Furthermore, he has dismantled the barriers of nation, race, and religion to realize a new world peace, founding the Abel UN, the Universal Peace Federation, and is working tirelessly to realize the ideal of a borderless family of humanity in 185 countries worldwide.
I hope that the readers who encounter these words will establish the true values of life that humanity must pursue, form true families, and become the protagonists in realizing a true peaceful world in the new millennium as owners of Cheon Il Guk. *

When you stand in such a decisive position, you must truly have the confidence that nothing can be done without you. Do you understand? "Yes." 
Even though you are women, you must resolve to go with such hope. That history is alive. When you think about such things.... In the past, when the teacher heard reports that someone was waiting for him in a lonely place because they heard rumors that he was passing by, and when he saw them, he thought, wow, is it something from 20 or 30 years ago, and when he heard reports that they were now active as the center of the sailors in that area, he was pleased. A Japanese woman and an American man became a couple, and under the guidance of a Japanese woman, they achieved such results. That is a result achieved by a Japanese, not by an American. Such results achieved by a Japanese are not just Japanese results. They are results created by the teacher. 
The Purpose of Raising Japanese Women Members
Therefore, when Japanese people come to praise the position you are standing in as great, when it is reported in the newspapers once, twice, or several times, everyone will understand at once. When that happens, wow, there were such women, women who left world records as sailors. It's not Yon-sama, Yon-sama. (Laughter) 
On land, everyone is lost and flocking like crazy because of Yon-sama, but they are indifferent to you, right? Don't feel disappointed because no one looks back. Look 10 or 20 years later. You will remain, but Yon-sama will only be a moment. He will disappear after 1 or 2 years. Rather than such a person, Japanese women who can freely move the rights of the sea, even without Japanese men, when they are called the owners of the maritime rights, Japan will never disappear from the earth as a maritime nation. That's a logical result. 
What is the purpose of raising Japanese women to achieve? It's about how to plant the foundation of the maritime rights that have been done so far into the world of sailors. When that happens, even from a leading standard, you are undoubtedly the ancestors who developed history. When that is recognized by everyone, your history becomes material for university professors of world maritime rights to learn and teach. When that happens, what will happen to Japan? 
Japan is now retreating in maritime rights. In places like Cape Town in Africa, where no one in the world goes, they thought the captain was Japanese, but everything was taken away by Koreans. Japan has now reached a standard of living comparable to Westerners, so they think they don't have to live such miserable lives.... That's fine temporarily, but if there are people who make efforts for 10, 20 years or more, Japan's future will be blocked. Who is developing that? 
If you continue this work, even 20 or 30 years later, if your descendants are lined up, when they become Japanese captains in the world, they will automatically become teachers at maritime elementary, middle, and high schools. Everyone graduated from university, right? Raise your hand if you're a university graduate. There were over forty, right? Including those who graduated from junior colleges. You all have enough qualifications to be teachers, so wow, if such people become queens of the world of sailors, when a school of such queens is established, when that happens, when you become a mother better than the father and mother of the students of that school, when you think about the traditional mission of mothers to make their sons and daughters successful, think about how that effect will spread worldwide and create the foundation. 
Small Japan, with its four islands, what path will it take in the future? It's surrounded by powerful countries, where will it go? Japan is more miserable than Korea. Korea can go anywhere on the continent. They are trained. They can go to Mongolia.... If they say they will go to Mongolia within a month, they don't need a visa. They can go anywhere without being guided. 
Even if the waves of the Tsushima Strait are high and dangerous, for sailors, it's an interesting place. If they want to smuggle into Japan, they can do it anytime. How many hours does it take to go from here to Fukuoka in Kyushu? Four hours? "It takes an hour and a half." An hour and a half? "It takes three hours." Well, there are various things. (Laughter) With a fast boat, it takes an hour and a half.... "It takes two hours and 55 minutes from Busan." How long from here? "From here, you have to go by bus...." (Laughter) How can you go by bus? "You have to go to Busan to take it." There's a ship going to Fukuoka from here, isn't there? 
There was a ferry coming the other day, wasn't there? "Yes." It takes just 2 hours, within 2 hours. It's like visiting a neighbor's house. Why can't you come and go? If you become sailors, 'Yes, I'll be back soon....' (Laughter) There's no problem. You can call your mother and father on your cell phone, since they can't check everything you use personally, you can contact them and tell them to come to such and such a cape to meet and share something good instead of dinner and say 'Goodbye.' (Laughter) Passing through the surroundings of a splendidly beautiful maritime city, passing through the very center of a beautiful city, think about it. Everyone will be fascinated. 
Wow! It's not just once. If you do it once or twice and it becomes a good thing for the country, even if you break the law in reality, 10 or 20 years later, they will thank you for forming a result that couldn't be formed by national borders 10 or 20 years ago. 
The teacher did the same, right? He sent Ishikawa-san to Japan for missionary work on a smuggling ship, right? Even though he was caught once or twice and detained in Omura detention center, 'Still, go, you rascal! If you have decided as a man, you can't stand before heaven without achieving results.' He sent him in a position like forcibly sending him, and within a week, he evangelized, and who is living now? Do you know who? Ishii's wife. Tomiko. You don't even know that? That's not even the issue. 
The Starting Point of History is Made in Places No One Likes
The starting point of history is made in places no one likes. The sea is not liked by anyone as a woman. You don't think of it as a base for creating a masterpiece model, do you? Do you understand? "Yes." 
Hey, Inoue! Inoue (井上) means a house above a well. (Laughter) If you don't know water well every day, it's a big deal. You have to protect it cleanly. Because of the name, you have a personality that can like anywhere in the maritime rights. Inoue, say it. "Inoue!" (Laughter) Because you've experienced various things, if you speak it in Korean, you'll get confused about what happened, (Laughter) because the pronunciation isn't clear.... (Laughter) If you speak it in Japanese, everyone will understand it without missing a word, and their expressions will become excellent. (Laughter) Wow! Inoue-sama is training to handle the public with words like that! Even the teacher can't help but be surprised. (Laughter) Applaud. (Applause) 
In the future maritime rights.... There are about 4,200 to 4,300 islands here. Japanese people want to take those islands and occupy Asian countries. Ah, women can go back and forth across borders day or night without any problem. When crossing the border to sell fish, when they say they have a sister there and are bringing some fish to sell, even if they are caught with 50 fish, if they say they are bringing it to give to a beggar, if they say they are going to give it to their sister or cousin, they are allowed to go because it's not bad. (Laughter) 
Once you go, you can make a path to go forever. Because Unification Church members, female members, male members, and child members do such things normally, when they become kings who digest borders, they become kings of the world's central kingdom, which is a natural result. Don't you think so? "I think so." Do you think so, or don't you think so? "I think so." It's okay if you don't think so. (Laughter)  
From now on, Korean women will say, 'Why do they make all these boats and hand them over to Japanese women who have completed the preparation of sailors....' It costs over 100 million. Even so, it's not like a bank asking for interest, it's just given away, so if you do such things, you shouldn't do it, and.... Even old grandmothers say, 'Yes, Korean women can do it better than Japanese women, Korean women are stronger.' Are Korean women stronger when compared to Japanese women? "Yes." 
Wherever you go, you have no choice but to rely on the embassy, to be guided, but Koreans, both women and men, and even children, never go to the embassy. (Laughter) People who rely on the embassy to achieve something in this country can't do anything. Koreans develop everything on their own. Japanese people carry the red flag and line up behind it, gathering a few people on one side of the road saying it's a big deal, but Koreans don't come until 10 minutes before the gathering time. (Laughter) When there are about 5 minutes left, they all appear from somewhere with good faces and start talking proudly, and it never ends, but Japanese people can't even see it as a group. It's hard to line up in front and back, and they can't even enjoy sightseeing, and if they are chased by time and have to run, it's a big deal. 
Koreans don't do such things. If they say they are going somewhere, they make sure to research the roads, shortcuts, and small paths the day before, and if it takes an hour to go officially, they research and go to a place where they can go in 15 minutes. That's how the personalities of Japanese and Koreans differ. 
Even when teaching language, in places like Africa or South America, if you go....
When it comes to learning Spanish, Koreans can do anything after a year and a half. Even if it takes five years for a Japanese person, they will lose to a Korean woman who has been learning for a year and a half. This is because Korean characters, as I mentioned, can be used to write 90% of the language, whereas Japanese characters cover less than 30%. Even pronouncing "McDonald's" requires saying "McDonald's," but they end up saying "Makudonarudo." (Laughter) Who understands that? Koreans write it down in their notebooks and memorize it quickly.

That's why it's interesting in that aspect. Once they hear something, by morning they know it all, speak it, and are determined to fully understand and learn it. If you ask them to teach you two things, they are happy to teach you. Even if you ask a busy girl passing by to teach you, she'll say, "Wow, that's great," and teach you. The next day, she'll say, "What you taught me yesterday means this," and will pronounce it all correctly. The next day, she'll teach you four things. Even four things will work. If ten things work, they'll buy a book like a translation guide and get guidance. So even if they memorize the entire book, they finish a 50-page or 40-page book in a month, even if they do two pages a day.

What will you do? Do you think you'll lose to a Korean woman or win? "I will win." (Laughter) So, you are bound to win. Even if a Korean woman is excellent, a first-year student cannot surpass a fifth-year student after three to five years of training. They will lose right away. So, in this time when everyone dislikes the sea, men and women alike, you, graduates of Japanese universities who have married Koreans...

In the future, coming to Korea will be difficult. As an enemy country of Japan, if there were no Unification Church ideology, it would be impossible for Koreans to marry Japanese even after ten thousand years of prayer. Because the Unification ideology is great, once they know that, even if everyone becomes enemies centered on national borders, they want to digest it all and come and go, so they don't consider crossing it a problem. When comparing with Japanese women and living in the same place, trying together, will they lose to Japanese women or win? They won't lose.

Korean Language Acquisition Ability

Also, it's the same for men. Because they communicate well, it's easy to become diplomats. Their pronunciation is good. No matter how much a Japanese person stays for ten years, if you look at Inoue-san, they can't understand 30%. You all would be the same, right? It's not certain, is it? In that aspect, Koreans have good pronunciation among the three countries of China, Japan, and Korea, so during war or diplomacy, the interpreters are Koreans. After staying in the field for about ten years, they won't lose to locals. Even when making phone calls, they won't lose. Koreans living in Japan are like that, right? After staying for about three years, they speak so well that it's hard to distinguish in normal conversation. So, this pronunciation, this language given by God is great.

And even if they use adverbs or adjectives in double or triple layers, they can interpret it. Because they interpret it right away, their brains are active, secreting a lot, so they are smart. That's why they say Japanese should never marry Koreans. Recently, Hyoryu! "Yes." Didn't you say your mother-in-law was surprised when you said Mr. Kim? Because they said not to marry a Korean, when asked what the surname was, they said Mr. Kim, and she was surprised, right? "Ah, yes." (Laughter)

That's how it is. When connected with Koreans, they can't keep up. It's a small island. When they go back and forth over large continents like Manchuria, they quickly think that Japanese won't do. So, even if they are the same sailors, when they learn about the maritime rights connecting continents like Korea, it's more connected to the world than sailing around Japan's four islands. From that perspective, what is the future outlook of the teacher's plan to conquer the world of global sailors centered on Japanese women? What do you think? Is it great? "It's great."

What does "subarashii" (すばらしい; great) mean? The character "su" means it has increased speed, so they think of it as "speedbarashii." It means the fastest. When you add "su" to "takai" (たかい; high), it means very high. When you say "subarashii," it means it's clear and there's nothing more to desire. In such weather, don't you say "subarashii"? When it's completely clear weather, excellent weather, you say "subarashii weather." It includes double meanings.

When you think about such things, even when learning Japanese, when you say it's interesting, think of "omoshiroi" (おもしろい; interesting) as interesting. When you say "omoshiroi," there's "omoguroi" (since "shiroi" means white, he humorously adds "kuroi" meaning black). (Laughter) (*From here, he speaks in Japanese) Also, when you say interesting, it means living in America, going to a better place than Korea, so it's interesting, living in America, isn't that what it means? Even when criticized, it has value.

So, do you think you met the teacher well or not? "We met well." The teacher was about to cough and didn't want to talk to you, but looking at it quietly, he thought he should say a word, so he talked, and today, should we go back or tomorrow? "Tomorrow."

The people brought here said they would return in three days, so they thought they would be taken back by helicopter without being sent back alone in three days, but should the teacher go out to sea or not?

The teacher has a hoarse voice and a cough, should he go out to sea or not? "You shouldn't go out." Today, I thought it would be good to take Inoue on a boat, but who are the women who can train Inoue? You can't miss a day of training.

Then, if you drop one person in the teacher's place, you can take two people. So if you tell them to go here and there, since they already know the possibility of catching fish, if they catch even one, they'll feel good, but if they catch none, won't they feel bad, these people here?

Women need to learn self-defense to board a boat

Did Yang Chang-sik testify yesterday in America? "No." Do you want to hear the testimony? "Yes." Ah, since America is a big country, how many hours would it take to testify? (Laughter)

How long does it take to fly, going from here to America, and Japanese planes are at the peak. When time is late, "Ah, I want to make them testify, but I can't." Aunt with Soviet ancestors, have you heard that sister's testimony? Come out, quickly. "Yes?" Yes, come quickly. (Applause)

I called her out to test what kind of determination the sister who received training the other day has, and since she came back to receive training again, what kind of determination she has. Is she a manly woman or a womanly woman? (Laughter) "I'm a manly woman." (Laughter)

When you become a captain in the future, you need to board a womanly man if you're a manly woman. If you become rough and shout "Wow!" when boarding, even a male captain might run away. That's why you need to learn karate.

There are many such cases. If you have a full load and the money amounts to tens of thousands of dollars, they might follow and throw all the women out, and if only three people go up, will they throw ten women into the sea or not?

That's why you need to learn martial arts at night. You need to learn self-defense. Got it? Since you're like a man, no one will look at you carelessly. "Wow, don't come near me, I do martial arts, karate, so I'll go into the sea," if you say this, they won't rush in.

Japanese Wife's Testimony

Look over there. It's a Soviet woman's face. Is your ancestor a Korean of Soviet descent? "No, my great-grandfather was a Soviet person." So that's right. It's really Soviet, Soviet. If your great-grandfather is of Soviet descent, you're really a Soviet woman. Now, tell us. When asked why you came back, to help everyone, if you say you came because you want to become a better sailor than me when the teacher comes, "Oh, I really don't have time, it's past eight, it's past meal time, oh, I don't know." I'm also a mood person. (Laughter) I called because I thought testifying is better than eating. Do well. (Testimony by Harada Keiko, who completed the 40-day special training for Korean-Japanese wives as marine leaders and is working as an assistant instructor in the marine providence team)

"……I had to go, but I was worried that my child would be concerned when he heard that his mom was going to Yeosu, so he was teary-eyed and talked about cartoons he saw on TV, trying to make me laugh, and seeing that, my heart hurt a lot. Do I really have to go to this extent?"

You shouldn't come! (Laughter) "……When I saw my brother always singing energetically in front and leading the whole group, I thought this was the atmosphere of the early church. I heard various testimonies from the deaconess, but many seniors who directly served Father don't testify much. Even if you ask, they seem to want to keep it to themselves, not telling much about it…"

Now, if they don't talk, ask why they don't. (Laughter) Ah, if you're a senior, you should talk, then. You can't not do that. Is this time, this kind of time, a good time or a bad time? "It's a good time." These are contents that can't be understood even after a thousand years of research. Experience is necessary. Go ahead!

"Senior families really suffered, but they had the opportunity to directly serve Father, and I was really envious of that one thing. Feeling the early church atmosphere centered on my brother was so good."

I'm the big brother. (Laughter) Isn't that right?

"……I really felt the heart with which the captains educated us. I thought it was just about driving the boat well, but it wasn't. Through that, I realized Father was like that too. He wanted to give us many blessings, but we had to set indemnity conditions for the responsibility humans must fulfill, and he had no choice but to give us those contents. I realized that if we don't take that path, God can't give us the blessings He wants to give us because Satan will accuse us."

Applaud, applaud. (Applause)

"It would be nice if we could choose to take that path willingly, but since we can't, Father had no choice but to give us those contents forcibly. When I think about how painful it must have been for him, I felt sorry for having complaints while living in the church. I realized that Father was listening to all my complaints, and how painful it must have been for him to hear them. I want to fulfill the given responsibility with a joyful and grateful heart."

So, I couldn't help but come here. Please take care of me. "Yes, please take care of me." (Laughter)

Did you have lunch, breakfast? "I haven't eaten yet." You must be hungry. Well, then! (Bow)

Ah, the weather is nice. "The climate is cold." The climate is cold? "Yes, the wind is cold." Ah, it's winter now. It should be cold. (Applause) *
